zhes gsungs /
de yang chos thams cad kyi snang stong skyon med kyi cha gnyis ka ma lus pa la 'khrul pa'i dri ma bag chags dang bcas pa zad pas /
yul can gcig gi cha shas kyis kyang /
yul thams cad kyi snang stong gnyis cig car du rtag tu mngon sum gyis gzigs pa'i ye shes ni 'bras bu sangs rgyas kyi sa'i khyad chos yin la /
gnyis snang 'khrul pa'i cha phra zhing phra ba dngos su sbyong ba'i rim pa rnams gsang sngags bla med kho na la yod pas /
rje bdag nyid chen pos kyang sngags kyi dpyad pa dgung lo nga drug gi dus su rdzogs /
pha rol tu phyin pa'i dpyad pa snga mo nas rdzogs rgyu yin pa la /
yang dag mtha' mngon du byed tshul gyi dka' gnad gsang sngags kyi spyod pa'i skabs shig la rag las pas de yang nga drug gi lo la rdzogs pa yin pas /
'di la sngon chad gzhan gyis ma myong ba'i mdo sngags kyi lam mngon du byed tshul gyi go ba chen po yod pa red /
sems can gyi dus su blo gcig gis bden gnyis cig car du mngon sum du rtogs mi nus kyang /
gang zag gcig gis bden gnyis la dus gcig tu mngon sum gyi nges pa 'dren thub pa mthong lam thob nas 'byung /
de'i sngon du nges 'byung byang sems kyis zin pa'i sgo nas gong du bshad pa ltar gyi chos rnams ming rkyang btags yod tsam gyi snang ba skyon med la nges pa drangs pas /
snang ba des stong pa mi sgrib par ma zad rang bzhin gyis stong pa de gsal bar byed cing /
stong pa des kyang snang ba de mi 'gog par ma zad bya byed 'thad pa'i snang ba de gsal bar byas pa'i phyir te /
chos rnams ltos med rang dbang gis stong pa yin pa ni gzhan la ltos nas grub par snang ba 'dis shes shing 'di la thug /
ltos grub kyi snang ba thams cad 'thad pa ni ltos med rang dbang gis stong pa kho na la rag las pa'i phyir /
de ltar snang stong gcig la nges pa drangs pa'i dus su gnyis ka la nges pa 'drongs thub pa nam byung ba de'i tshe /
slob dpon chen po klu sgrub dang 'phags pa lha gnyis kyi dgongs pa mthar thug rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul du sangs rgyas bskyangs dang zla ba grags pa zhi ba lha gsum gyis gsal bar mdzad pa'i bka' srol zhing 'dir chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha pa chen pos legs par bshad pa'i snying po stong dang rten 'byung don gcig tu rtogs pa'i dbu ma'i lam bzang mngon sum du rnyed par 'gyur ba yin no / /
lam gtso las /
gzhan yang snang bas yod mtha' sel ba dang / /
stong pas med mtha' sel zhing stong pa nyid / /
rgyu dang 'bras bur 'char ba'i tshul shes na / /

zhes gsungs pa'i snang bas yod mtha' sel ba dang /

de ni lugs gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i dka' gnad kyang yin no / /
chos rnams dus rtag tu rang bzhin gyis grub pas stong stong pa'i mu nas gzhan la brten nas rgyu 'bras sogs de dang der snang bar yid ches na stong nyid rgyu 'bras su 'char ba yin no / /
de yang stong nyid bsgom pas sngon las 'bras bsgom pa las kyang lhag pa'i rgyu 'bras la nges pa cher rnyed nas nang gi nyon mongs chung du song zhing /
phyi'i spyod pa rnam par dag tu song na lta sgom gnad du song ba'i rtags yang dag yin zhes bdag gi bla ma rin po ches yang nas yang du gsungs /
'on kyang da dung yul stong nyid mngon sum du ma rtogs pas /

de 'dra'i dpyad pa rang stobs kyis drangs pa'i lus sems shin sbyangs kyi bde bas zin pa'i ting 'dzin nam rgyud la skyes pa na sbyor lam drod thob cing /

de ltar mthong lam thob nas kyang / /
mthong spang gi dngos gnyen byed pa'i bar chad med lam dang /

rang gi sems kyi chos nyid @# / /
mthong spang dang bral ba'i bral cha mngon sum du ma rtogs pa dang /

de bzhin du sgom lam sa bcu la yang /

ces gsungs /
de yang gong du dam bcas pa ltar tshig don de skad rdzogs par smra ba po rang nyid lung rtogs kyi bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi bdag po mtshan 'di zhes bya bar zhal gyis bzhes nas /
brtsams pa mthar phyin pa'i dge bas 'gro kun zhi bde thar pa la 'jug pa'i sgo mi 'dra ba gnyis su med pa'i gcig pu de kho na nyid ji bzhin rtogs pa'i lam 'di thob nas /
thabs khyad par can gyi grogs dang ma bral bas myur du sgrib gnyis kyi g.yul las rgyal ba'i rgyal ba sangs rgyas thob par gyur cig ces bsngo bar mdzad do / /
mdor na zhi sgo gcig tu gsungs pa 'di 'dra ba la des pa phul du byung ba gnyis drang rgyu yod pa lam rim chen mor gsungs pa ltar nges par mdzad dgos /
de yang 'di ltar sangs rgyas lta zhog 'khor ba las grol ba'i thar pa tsam thob pa la yang lta ba 'di med thabs med par dngos su bstan pa ltar nges nas 'bad pa chen pos thabs du ma'i sgo nas lta ba rnam dag 'di ci rnyed byed pa dang /
theg pa che chung gi khyad par 'byed pa'i chos ni kun rdzob byang chub kyi sems rin po che kho na yin par don gyis bstan ba ltar nges nas nus pa ci yod kyi sgo nas sems rin po che de gsar du bskyed pa dang /
des zin pa'i sbyin sogs spyod phyogs rnams la lhag par yang gdams pa'i mthil du bzung nas bslab par bya dgos so / /
de ltar lam phra zhing phra ba nas ma lus par thabs shes zung 'jug tu nyams su len pa 'di ni /

nyams len 'dis ni rang gang la ldan pa'i skyes bu mchog de /
bar du srid zhi'i mtha' gnyis gang du yang mi lhung bar bsrung nas /

sras bcas rgyal ba rnams kyis bdag nyid 'dul ba la mchog tu bsngags pa blo bzang thub dbang rdo rje 'chang dngos rje bla ma blo bzang rnam grol dpal bzang po nas da lam skabs su babs pas bshad khrid gtong dgos tshul gyi bka' phebs byung ba dang rmi ltas kyang bzang ba bcas /
de 'phral phran rang nas rtse gcig pa'i gsol 'debs byas te /
dben gnas ke'u tshang ri khrod du bshad pa gang shes zhus par de skabs bla ma rin po che nas rtsa ba'i sa bcad dang yan lag gi 'phros bshad phal cher la zin bris mdzad 'dug pa slar yang nged la de nyid tshig don cha tshang bar gung bsgrigs dgos zhes bka' stsal pa na /
nged rang la de lta bu'i gzungs spobs gang yang ma mchis rung /
dus gsum rgyal ba'i mkhyen @# / /
brtse nus gsum yon tan 'phran las dang bcas pa'i ngo bo thugs rje chen pos bskyod pa'i thabs mkhas kyi mdzad pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgo nas bdag cag rjes su bzung ba'i bka' drin mtshungs zla ma mchis pa rje bla ma srid zhi'i gtsug rgyan yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag don gyi slad du mtshan nas smas te bdag gri mkhan rin po che rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi bdag po rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang dngos rje btsun blo bzang ye shes bstan pa rab rgyas dpal bzang po dang /
rje btsun rtsa ba'i bla ma blo bzang rnam grol dpal bzang po dang /
sgrub brtson dem pa rje btsun rgya mtsho dbang phyug dpal bzang po bcas kyi zhabs drung nas 'di kha'i bshad khrid rgyas par thob cing de dus kyi man ngag dang rang 'grel yang gsal sgron me la gzhi byas te phyogs gcig tu 'god pa po ni zung 'jug bla ma rin po che rnams kyi skyabs 'og tu tshud nas yun ring lon zhing thugs rje dang bka' drin kho nas 'tsho ba /
gzhon nu'i dus nas bla ma lha mchag la mi phyed pa'i dad gus cung zed thob pa bla ma dang lhan cig gnas pa rked tshang sprul ming 'dzin pa blo bzang 'jam dbyangs smon lam gyis bka' gdams bstan pa'i chu 'go r+wa sgreng rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyi bla brang dge 'phel gling du dwang bas sbyar pa'i yi ge pa ni rang gi slab ma dben sa pa dge slong rnam rgyal bkra shis kyis bgyis pa'o / /
sgrub par mi 'os bshad pa'i tshogs mchis na / /
gzhung lugs gdams par shar bas bsal du gsol / /
legs par bshad pas 'gro rgyud byin brlabs nas / /
'jam dpal snying po'i bstan pa rgyas par shog / / /
